Slide 12: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Entertainment Areas">Mga Lugar ng Libangan</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The park is a beautiful place for playing.">Ang parke ay magandang pook para sa paglalaro.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The words 'park' and 'playground' are common nouns.">Ang 'parke' at 'laruan' ay mga pambalana sa wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Here we run around and play with our friends.">Dito tayo tumatakbo at nakikipaglaro sa mga kaibigan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="If the park has a specific name, it is proper.">Kung ang parke ay may tiyak na pangalan, ito ay pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: 'Koronadal Plaza' is a proper noun.">Halimbawa: 'Koronadal Plaza' ay isang pangngalang pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Even 'SG Farm sa Tupi' is a proper noun.">Maging ang 'SG Farm sa Tupi' ay pantangi rin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's always remember the correct way to write it.">Lagi nating tandaan ang wastong pagsulat nito.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Use a capital letter at the start of each word!">Gumamit ng malaking titik sa simula ng bawat salita!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of entertainment: park (park - pambalana), Luneta Park (proper)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Libangan: parke (park - pambalana), Luneta Park (proper)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="entertainment">Libangan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="park (park - pambalana), Luneta Park (proper)">parke (park - pambalana), Luneta Park (proper)</span>

Slide 13: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Sentence Analysis">Pagsusuri sa Pangungusap</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's analyze the place nouns in sentences.">Suriin natin ang mga pook sa pangungusap.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Statement: 'We went to a big school.'">Pahayag: 'Pumunta kami sa isang malaking paaralan.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place here is 'school' which is a common noun.">Ang pook dito ay 'paaralan' na isang pambalana.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Another statement: 'We are studying in Koronadal.'">Isa pang pahayag: 'Kami ay nag-aaral sa Koronadal.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place here is 'Koronadal' which is a proper noun.">Ang pook dito ay 'Koronadal' na isang pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is the specific name of a city in Timog Cotabato.">Ito ay tiyak na ngalan ng lungsod sa Timog Cotabato.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="So it starts with the capital letter C.">Kaya nagsisimula ito sa malaking titik na C.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Is it easy to identify these places in sentences?">Madali lang bang matukoy ang mga pook na ito?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Analysis: school (common noun) vs. Koronadal (proper noun)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsusuri: paaralan (common noun) vs. Koronadal (proper noun)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Analysis">Pagsusuri</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="school (common noun) vs. Koronadal (proper noun)">paaralan (common noun) vs. Koronadal (proper noun)</span>

Slide 14: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Capitalization Rule">Panuntunan sa Malaking Titik</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Why is the capital letter important for proper nouns?">Bakit mahalaga ang malaking titik sa pantangi?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It indicates the specific and unique name of a place.">Ito ay nagpapakita ng tiyak na ngalan ng pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="If we write 'pilipinas' in lowercase, it is wrong.">Kung isusulat natin ang 'pilipinas', ito ay mali.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It must be written as 'Pilipinas' with a capital P.">Dapat itong isulat na 'Pilipinas' na may malaking P.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Likewise for 'lawa ng sebu', it must be 'Lawa ng Sebu'.">Gayundin sa 'lawa ng sebu', dapat ay 'Lawa ng Sebu'.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Capital letter L and capital letter S are both required.">Malaki ang titik L at malaki rin ang titik S.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct spelling and grammar in our language.">Ito ang wastong bantas at baybay sa ating wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Practice writing this correctly every single day!">Sanayin ang sarili sa pagsulat nito araw-araw!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Proper Writing: wrong: lake sebu -&gt; right: lake sebu">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Wastong Pagsulat: mali: lawa ng sebu -> tama: Lawa ng Sebu</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Proper Writing">Wastong Pagsulat</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: lake sebu -&gt; right: lake sebu">mali: lawa ng sebu -> tama: Lawa ng Sebu</span>

Slide 15: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Threats Around Us">Pambalana sa Ating Paligid</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Look outside your window right now.">Tumingin ka sa labas ng inyong bintana ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What general places can you observe out there?">Ano-anong mga pangkalahatang pook ang iyong nakikita?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Maybe there is a road, field, river, or houses.">Maaaring may kalsada, bukid, ilog, o kabahayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="These words represent general types of places.">Ang mga salitang ito ay mga pangkalahatang pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="So they are common nouns in our language.">Kaya sila ay mga pangngalang pambalana sa wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Write them using lowercase letters only.">Isulat ang mga ito gamit ang maliit na titik lamang.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We do not need to capitalize the start of the word.">Hindi natin kailangang lakihan ang simula ng salita.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is a basic rule in our grammar lessons!">Ito ay isang pangunahing tuntunin sa ating balarila!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Ominous: road, field, mountain">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pambalana: kalsada (road), bukid (field), bundok (mountain)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Ominous">Pambalana</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="road, field, mountain">kalsada (road), bukid (field), bundok (mountain)</span>

Slide 16: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Heroes and Their Places">Mga Bayani at Kanilang Pook</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Many places are named after our national heroes.">Maraming pook ang ipinangalan sa mga bayani natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Examples: 'Rizal Street' or 'Town of Bonifacio'.">Halimbawa: 'Kalye Rizal' o 'Bayan ng Bonifacio'.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="These historical places are proper nouns.">Ang mga pook na ito ay mga pangngalang pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="A capital letter is needed due to the specific name.">Kailangan ang malaking titik dahil may tiyak na ngalan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Matteo's cousin was born in Koronadal, Timog Cotabato.">Ang pinsan ni Matteo ay ipinanganak sa Koronadal, Timog Cotabato.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Both 'Koronadal' and 'Timog Cotabato' are proper nouns.">Ang 'Koronadal' at 'Timog Cotabato' ay parehong pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="They start with the capital letters K and T.">Sila ay nagsisimula sa malalaking titik na K at T.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This shows respect to these important places!">Ito ay nagpapakita ng paggalang sa mga pook na ito!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Heroes and Places: Rizal (hero) -&gt; Kalye Rizal (proper noun of place)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Bayani at Pook: Rizal (bayani) -> Kalye Rizal (proper noun of place)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Heroes and Places">Bayani at Pook</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Rizal (hero) -&gt; Kalye Rizal (proper noun of place)">Rizal (bayani) -> Kalye Rizal (proper noun of place)</span>

Slide 17: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Exercise: Finding a Place">Pagsasanay: Paghahanap ng Pook</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's play a game of finding places today.">Maglaro tayo ng paghahanap ng mga pook ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Read: 'Matteo went to the big market.'">Basahin: 'Pumunta si Matteo sa malaking palengke.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Where did Matteo go in our sentence?">Saan pumunta si Matteo sa ating pangungusap?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="He went to the 'market' which is a general place.">Pumunta siya sa 'palengke' na isang pangkalahatang pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The word 'market' is a common noun of place.">Ang salitang 'palengke' ay pangngalang pambalana.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is written using a lowercase letter p.">Isinusulat ito gamit ang maliit na titik p.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Try to find other places in different stories!">Subukan mong maghanap ng pook sa iba pang kwento!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is a great way to practice your skills!">Ito ay isang mahusay na paraan ng pagsasanay!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Training: market (common noun - place)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsasanay: palengke (common noun - place)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Training">Pagsasanay</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="market (common noun - place)">palengke (common noun - place)</span>

Slide 18: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Training: Specific Area">Pagsasanay: Tiyak na Pook</span>
  [Current Image: images/filipino_w1_img3.png]
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's read another sentence in our language.">Basahin natin ang isa pang pangungusap sa wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Statement: 'They went on vacation to Baguio City.'">Pahayag: 'Sila ay nagbakasyon sa Lungsod ng Baguio.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What is the specific place mentioned in the statement?">Ano ang tiyak na pook na binanggit sa pahayag?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The specific place is 'Baguio City' in Luzon.">Ang tiyak na pook ay 'Lungsod ng Baguio' sa Luzon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is a proper noun in our language.">Ito ay isang pangngalang pantangi sa ating wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It starts with a capital letter L and capital B.">Nagsisimula ito sa malaking titik L at malaking B.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This shows the specific name of the city.">Ito ay nagpapakita ng tiyak na ngalan ng lungsod.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Can you write it down on your paper right now?">Maaari mo ba itong isulat sa iyong papel ngayon?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Training: City of Baguio (proper noun - Slide 19: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Exercise: Right or Wrong?">Pagsasanay: Tama o Mali?</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's check the spelling of the following places.">Suriin natin ang pagsulat ng mga sumusunod na pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Statement: 'He lives in barangay san Juan.'">Pahayag: 'Nakatira siya sa barangay san Juan.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Is there a mistake in writing this place name?">Mayroon bang pagkakamali sa pagsulat ng pook na ito?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Yes, 'barangay san Juan' should be a proper noun.">Oo, ang 'barangay san Juan' ay dapat maging pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It must be written as 'Barangay San Juan' with capitals.">Dapat itong isulat na 'Barangay San Juan' na malaki.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Capital B, capital S, and capital J are all needed.">Malaki ang titik B, malaki ang S, at malaki ang J.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct way to write our barangay name.">Ito ang tamang paraan ng pagsulat ng ating barangay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Always be careful with capital letters in your writing!">Palaging maging maingat sa malalaking titik sa pagsulat!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Training: wrong: barangay san juan -&gt; right: barangay San Juan">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsasanay: mali: barangay san juan -> tama: Barangay San Juan</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Training">Pagsasanay</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: barangay san juan -&gt; right: barangay San Juan">mali: barangay san juan -> tama: Barangay San Juan</span>

Slide 20: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Letter Misuse">Maling Paggamit ng Titik</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid writing common nouns with capital letters.">Iwasan ang pagsusulat ng pambalana sa malaking titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'We went to a Hospital.' (common noun capitalized)">Mali: 'Pumunta kami sa isang Ospital.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The word 'hospital' is just a common noun here.">Ang 'ospital' ay pambalana lamang sa pangungusap.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="So it should be written with a lowercase letter o.">Kaya dapat itong isulat sa maliit na titik o.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Correct: 'We went to a hospital.' (lowercase o)">Tama: 'Pumunta kami sa isang ospital.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Do not capitalize the letter if it is not specific.">Huwag lakihan ang titik kung hindi ito tiyak.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is a common mistake made by young learners.">Ito ay isang karaniwang pagkakamali ng mga bata.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make sure your letters are correct in your writing now!">Tiyakin na tama ang iyong mga titik sa pagsulat ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Wrong letter: wrong: Hospital -&gt; right: hospital">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Maling Titik: mali: Ospital -> tama: ospital</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong letter">Maling Titik</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: Hospital -&gt; right: hospital">mali: Ospital -> tama: ospital</span>

Slide 21: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Identifying Categories">Pagkilala sa mga Kategorya</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Do not confuse people or things with places.">Huwag ipagpalit ang tao o bagay sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The 'teacher' is a person; the 'school' is a place.">Ang 'guro' ay tao; ang 'paaralan' ay pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The 'book' is a thing; the 'library' is a place.">Ang 'aklat' ay bagay; ang 'aklatan' ay pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The 'doctor' is a person; the 'hospital' is a place.">Ang 'doktor' ay tao; ang 'ospital' ay pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Analyze carefully what the word is referring to.">Suriin nang mabuti kung ano ang tinutukoy ng salita.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Is it a location, or an object, or a person?">Ito ba ay isang lugar o kagamitan o tao?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Classifying into categories is an important skill.">Ang pag-uri sa kategorya ay mahalagang kasanayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This will help in understanding the meaning of words!">Makatutulong ito sa pag-unawa ng kahulugan ng salita!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Category: book (thing) vs. library (place)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Kategorya: aklat (bagay) vs. aklatan (pook - place)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Category">Kategorya</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="book (thing) vs. library (place)">aklat (bagay) vs. aklatan (pook - place)</span>

Slide 22: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Why Does Location Matter?">Bakit Mahalaga ang Pook?</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Places provide the setting for our stories.">Ang mga pook ay nagbibigay ng setting sa kwento.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is where all important events take place.">Dito nagaganap ang lahat ng mahahalagang pangyayari.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="In writing stories, we need to specify the place.">Sa pagsulat ng kwento, kailangan natin ang pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Specifying the place gives clarity to the reader.">Ang pagtukoy sa pook ay nagbibigay-linaw sa mambabasa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We can use either common or proper nouns.">Maaari nating gamitin ang pambalana o pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This depends on whether we want to be specific or not.">Depende ito kung nais nating maging tiyak o hindi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Use your knowledge to write a short story!">Gamitin ang iyong kaalaman upang sumulat ng kwento!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Share it with your teacher and classmates today!">Ibahagi ito sa iyong guro at mga kamag-aral ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Importance: Place answers the question: Where? (Where?)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Kahalagahan: Ang pook ay sumasagot sa tanong na: Saan? (Where?)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Importance">Kahalagahan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Place answers the question: Where? (Where?)">Ang pook ay sumasagot sa tanong na: Saan? (Where?)</span>

Slide 23: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Area Writing Guide">Gabay sa Pagsusulat ng Pook</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Here is a quick guide to writing places correctly.">Narito ang mabilis na gabay sa pagsusulat ng pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="First, determine if it is common or proper.">Una, alamin kung ito ay pambalana o pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Second, if it is proper, capitalize the first letter.">Pangalawa, kung ito ay pantangi, lakihan ang titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Third, if common, use lowercase first letters.">Pangatlo, kung pambalana, gamitin ang maliit na titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Fourth, make sure of the correct spelling of words.">Pang-apat, tiyakin ang tamang baybay ng mga salita.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: 'Lungsod ng San Pablo' has capital L and S.">Halimbawa: 'Lungsod ng San Pablo' ay may malaking L at S.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The connecting word 'ng' remains in lowercase.">Ang salitang 'ng' ay nananatiling maliit ang titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Follow this guide in your practice exercises today!">Sundan ang gabay na ito sa iyong mga pagsasanay ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of guide: Special -&gt; Upper case. Symbol -&gt; Lower case.">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Gabay: Pantangi -> Malaking titik. Pambalana -> Maliit na titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="guide">Gabay</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Special -&gt; Upper case. Symbol -&gt; Lower case.">Pantangi -> Malaking titik. Pambalana -> Maliit na titik.</span>

Slide 24: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Summary of Week One">Buod ng Unang Linggo</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Congratulations! You completed the slides for Week 1.">Binabati kita! Natapos mo ang mga slide sa Week 1.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We learned about common nouns of places.">Natutunan natin ang mga pangngalang pambalana sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We also learned about proper nouns of places.">Natutunan din natin ang pangngalang pantangi sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We discovered the correct use of capital letters.">Nalaman natin ang wastong paggamit ng malaking titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We used examples from our local community.">Ginamit natin ang mga halimbawa sa ating komunidad.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Are you ready to try the quiz and challenges?">Handa ka na bang subukan ang pagsusulit at hamon?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Show your skill in identifying these places!">Ipakita ang iyong galing sa pagtukoy ng mga pook!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Continue studying the Filipino language!">Ipagpatuloy ang pag-aaral ng wikang Filipino!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Remember: Place = Place. Unique = Certain. Predestination = Normal.">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Tandaan: Pook = Lugar. Pantangi = Tiyak. Pambalana = Karaniwan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Remember">Tandaan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Place = Place. Unique = Certain. Predestination = Normal.">Pook = Lugar. Pantangi = Tiyak. Pambalana = Karaniwan.</span>

Slide 1: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What is History?">Ano ang Kasaysayan?</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="History is not just simply old stories from the past.">Ang kasaysayan ay hindi lamang basta lumang kwento.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is the study of meaningful past events in lives.">Ito ay pag-aaral ng may-saysay na nakaraang yugto.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There are four important elements of history we study today.">May apat na mahahalagang elemento ang kasaysayan ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="These are the people, place, time, and the event itself.">Ito ang tao, lugar, panahon, at ang pangyayari.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It answers who, where, when, and what happened yonder.">Sinasagot nito ang sino, saan, kailan, at ano.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The unity of these elements creates the historical story.">Ang pagkakaisa ng mga ito ang bumubuo sa kwento.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim,   Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="History always takes place in a specific physical location.">Ang kasaysayan ay laging nagaganap sa isang lugar.</span> <span class="fil-sentence"   [Current Image: images/makabansa_w1_img1.png]

Slide 5: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The Element: Event">Ang Elemento: Pangyayari</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The event is the actual action or occurrence that happened.">Ang pangyayari ay ang mismong aksyon na naganap.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There are events that have deep meaning for a place.">May mga pangyayaring may malalim na saysay sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: the foundation of the first school in town.">Halimbawa: ang pagtatag ng unang paaralan sa bayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Or perhaps the historical battles fought for our freedom.">O di kaya ay ang labanan para sa kalayaan natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There are also celebrations like the local town festival.">Mayroon ding mga pagdiriwang tulad ng pista ng bayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="These events change the way of life of the citizens.">Ang mga ito ay nagbabago sa pamumuhay ng mamamayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Historians record these important events in their books.">Itinatala ito ng mga historyador sa kanilang aklat.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What is the most important historical event in your place?">Ano ang pinakamahalagang pangyayari sa inyong pook?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Element: Event: founding of the town, war, festival, declaration">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Elemento: Pangyayari: pagtatag ng bayan, digmaan, pista, deklarasyon</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Element: Event">Elemento: Pangyayari</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="founding of the town, war, festival, declaration">pagtatag ng bayan, digmaan, pista, deklarasyon</span>

Slide 6: Primary Sources: Artifacts
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How do we know the history of our local community?">Paano natin nalalaman ang kasaysayan ng komunidad?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We use primary sources during our historical research.">Gumagamit tayo ng mga primaryang batayan sa pagsusuri.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Artifacts are physical objects made and used in the past.">Ang artifact ay mga pisikal na kagamitan sa nakaraan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Examples: old clay pots, ancient coins, and old tools.">Halimbawa: lumang palayok, barya, at mga kasangkapan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="These physical objects do not lie about past human activities.">Ang mga ito ay hindi nagsisinungaling sa kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="They show us exactly how our ancestors lived their daily lives.">Ipinapakita nito kung paano namuhay ang mga ninuno.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We can observe these historical items in museums today.">Makikita natin ang mga ito sa mga museo ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Is there an old object preserved in your own house today?">Mayroon bang lumang kagamitan sa inyong sariling bahay?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Artifacts: old coins, pots, old furniture">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Artifacts: lumang barya (old coins), palayok (pots), lumang kasangkapan</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: Artifacts: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="old coins, pots, old furniture">lumang barya (old coins), palayok (pots), lumang kasangkapan</span>

Slide 8: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Secondary Sources in History">Secondary Sources sa Kasaysayan</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There are also secondary sources of history we can use.">Mayroon ding mga sekondaryang batayan sa kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" maunawaan ang paksa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Your teacher's stories about Rizal belong to this category.">Ang kwento ng iyong guro tungkol kay Rizal ay ganoon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Use both sources of data to keep your records accurate!">Gamitin ang parehong batayan upang maging tumpak ang tala!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" Slide 9: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The Importance of Timeline">Ang Kahalagahan ng Timeline</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="A timeline is a line that displays the sequence of time.">Ang timeline ay isang guhit na nagpapakita ng panahon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It arranges events in order from the earliest to the latest.">Inaayos nito ang mga pangyayari mula una hanggang huli.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We read the horizontal timeline from left to right in books.">Binabasa natin ang timeline mula kaliwa pakanan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: a timeline of a child growing up in the community.">Halimbawa: timeline ng paglaki ng isang bata sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="2018: born;   Example: Timeline: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="2018 (Born) -&gt; 2024 (Kinder) -&gt; 2026 (Grade 3)">2018 (Ipinanganak) -> 2024 (Kinder) -> 2026 (Grade 3)</span>

Slide 10: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The Origin of the Name">Ang Pinagmulan ng Pangalan</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Every barangay has a story behind its physical name.">Ang bawat barangay ay may kwento ng kanyang pangalan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Usually it originates from local plants, trees, or animals.">Karaniwan itong nagmula sa mga halaman o hayop.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="E.g., 'Kawayanan' the place.">O kaya ay 'San Jose' bilang parangal sa isang patron.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Some names also originate from local terms of indigenous people.">Mayroon ding nagmula sa mga lokal na salita ng katutubo.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Knowing the name is the start of respecting the local place.">Ang pag-alam sa pangalan ay simula ng paggalang sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It reflects the culture and natural resources of the place.">Sinasalamin nito ang kultura at likas na yaman ng pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What is the origin of the name of your own barangay?">Ano ang pinagmulan ng pangalan ng iyong sariling barangay?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Origin: Kawayanan (from bamboo), San Jose (from patron)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pinagmulan: Kawayanan (mula sa kawayan), San studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Origin">Pinagmulan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Kawayanan (from bamboo), San Jose (from patron)">Kawayanan (mula sa kawayan), San Jose (mula sa patron)</span>

Slide 11: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Oral History: Word of mouth">Oral History: Saling-bibig</span>
  [Current Image: images/makabansa_w1_img2.png]
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Not all history is written down in big books yonder.">Hindi lahat ng kasaysayan ay nakasulat sa aklat.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Some stories are passed down using the mouth and ears.">May mga kwentong isinasalin sa pamamagitan ng bibig.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We call this oral history or verbal storytelling in class.">Tinatawag natin itong oral history o saling-bibig.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Grandfathers and grandmothers tell stories to their children.">Ang mga lolo at lola ay nagkukuwento sa mga bata.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="They share how life was yonder during the old days of town.">Ibinabahagi nila kung paano ang buhay noong araw sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Even without books, we can preserve the community memories.">Kahit walang aklat, napananatili natin ang alaala.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This oral tradition is a valuable part of our local culture.">Ito ay isang mahalagang bahagi ng ating kultura.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Listen carefully when elders are sharing their memories!">Makinig nang mabuti kapag nagkukuwento ang nakatatanda!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Mouth to mouth: Grandparents&#x27; stories about the past.">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Saling-bibig: Mga kwento ng lolo at lola tungkol sa nakaraan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Mouth to mouth">Saling-bibig</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Grandparents&#x27; stories about the past.">Mga kwento ng lolo at lola tungkol sa nakaraan.</span>

Slide 15: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Guided Practice: The Review">Guided Practice: Ang Pagsusuri</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's analyze a short story of our local history.">Suriin natin ang isang kwento ng ating kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Read: 'Barangay San Jose was founded in the year 1950.'">Basahin: 'Itinatag ang Barangay San Jose noong 1950.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Identify the place mentioned in our statement yonder.">Tukuyin ang pook na binanggit sa ating pahayag.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place is 'Barangay San Jose' which is proper.">Ang pook ay 'Barangay San Jose' na isang pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Identify the time period mentioned in our statement.">Tukuyin ang panahon na binanggit sa ating pahayag.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The time is 'in 1950' which is a specific year.">Ang panahon ay 'noong 1950' na isang tiyak na taon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The founding is the event that has deep historical meaning.">Ang pagtatag ay ang pangyayaring may malalim na saysay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Did you find all three elements in your analysis today?">Nahanap mo ba ang tatlong elemento sa pagsusuri?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Analysis: Place -&gt; Barangay San Jose, Period -&gt; 1950, Event -&gt; Establishment">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsusuri: Pook -> Barangay San Jose, Panahon -> 1950, Pangyayari -> Pagtatag</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Analysis">Pagsusuri</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Place -&gt; Barangay San Jose, Period -&gt; 1950, Event -&gt; Establishment">Pook -> Barangay San Jose, Panahon -> 1950, Pangyayari -> Pagtatag</span>

Slide 16: Guided Practice: Primary vs Secondary
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's check the following sources of historical data.">Suriin natin ang mga sumusunod na batayan ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="If you find an old coin dated with the year 1900,">Kung nakakita ka ng lumang barya na may taong 1900,</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="this is a primary source (artifact) for the place.">ito ay isang primaryang batayan (artifact) sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="If you read the book 'History of Timog Cotabato' in class,">Kung binabasa mo ang aklat na 'Kasaysayan ng Timog Cotabato',</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="this is a secondary source in our history lesson today.">ito ay isang sekondaryang batayan sa ating aralin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The book was written by a researcher after studying coins.">Ang aklat ay isinulat ng mananaliksik pagkatapos.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Both sources of data are valuable for historical study.">Parehong mahalaga ang dalawang batayan sa kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Which would you prefer to examine: the coin or the book?">Alin ang mas nais mong suriin: barya o aklat?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Basis: old coin -&gt; primary, textbook -&gt; secondary">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Batayan: lumang barya -> primary, textbook -> secondary</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers.">Mahalagang magsanay nang regular at talakayin ang mga ideyang ito sa iyong mga kasamahan at guro.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Basis">Batayan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="old coin -&gt; primary, textbook -&gt; secondary">lumang barya -> primary, textbook -> secondary</span>

Slide 17: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Guided Practice: Area Timeline">Guided Practice: Timeline ng Pook</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's create a timeline for our local barangay hall.">Gumawa tayo ng timeline ng isang barangay hall.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="2000: The small barangay hall was founded in the place.">2000: Itinatag ang maliit na barangay hall sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="2010: The building was expanded and a clinic was added.">2010: Pinalawak ang gusali at nagdagdag ng klinika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="2020: A new sports complex was built next to the hall.">2020: Nagpatayo ng bagong sports complex sa tabi nito.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Notice the correct chronological order of the years yonder.">Pansinin ang tamang pagkakasunod-sunod ng mga taon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="From the earliest (2000) leading to the present (2020).">Mula sa pinakamaaga (2000) patungo sa kasalukuyan (2020).</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This shows the physical growth and development of the place.">Ipinapakita nito ang paglago at pag-unlad ng pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Copy this timeline structure into your own notebook now!">Kopyahin ang timeline na ito sa iyong sariling notebook!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Timeline: 2000 (Establishment) -&gt; 2010 (Clinic) -&gt; 2020 (Sports Complex)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Timeline: 2000 (Pagtatag) -> 2010 (Klinika) -> 2020 (Sports Complex)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: Timeline: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="2000 (Establishment) -&gt; 2010 (Clinic) -&gt; 2020 (Sports Complex)">2000 (Pagtatag) -> 2010 (Klinika) -> 2020 (Sports Complex)</span>

Slide 18: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Guided Practice: Logo Analysis">Guided Practice: Pagsusuri ng Logo</span>
  [Current Image: images/makabansa_w1_img3.png]
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's analyze the logo of a barangay near our school.">Suriin natin ang logo ng isang barangay sa tabi natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There is a drawing of three fish and a net in the middle.">May guhit ng tatlong isda at lambat sa gitna nito.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What is the meaning of the fish on this local logo?">Ano ang ibig sabihin ng mga isda sa logo ng pook?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It shows that fishing is the main source of livelihood there.">Ipinapakita nito na pangingisda ang kabuhayan doon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place is near a lake or sea, hence the fish symbol.">Ang pook ay malapit sa lawa o dagat kaya may isda.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This expresses the story of the people's way of life.">Ito ay naglalahad ng kwento ng pamumuhay ng tao.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is not just decoration; it holds a deep meaning yonder.">Ito ay hindi lamang palamuti; may malalim na saysay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Draw the logo of your own barangay on a clean sheet of paper!">Iguhit ang logo ng iyong barangay sa isang malinis na papel!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Logo Analysis: fish and nets -&gt; fishing livelihood">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsusuri ng Logo: isda at lambat -> kabuhayan sa pangingisda (fishing)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Logo Analysis">Pagsusuri ng Logo</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="fish and nets -&gt; fishing livelihood">isda at lambat -> kabuhayan sa pangingisda (fishing)</span>

Slide 19: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Misidentifying the Past">Maling Pagtukoy sa Nakaraan</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid treating ordinary past events as historical events.">Iwasan ang pagtrato sa ordinaryong bagay bilang kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'My eating of bread yesterday is part of history.'">Mali: 'Ang pagkain ko ng tinapay kahapon ay kasaysayan.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is just the past, but has no major significance to the town.">Ito ay nakaraan lamang, ngunit walang saysay sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="History must have a major and lasting impact on the community.">Ang kasaysayan ay dapat may malaking epekto sa lahat.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: the construction of the first bridge over the river.">Halimbawa: ang pagpapatayo ng unang tulay sa ilog.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This changed transport for the entire local community.">Ito ay binago ang transportasyon ng buong komunidad.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make sure the event is significant in your history logs!">Tiyakin na makabuluhan ang pangyayari sa iyong logs!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the true meaning of history in our social studies!">Ito ang totoong kahulugan ng kasaysayan sa atin!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Misidentification: past (past - ordinary) vs. history (history - significant)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Maling Pagtukoy: nakaraan (past - ordinary) vs. kasaysayan (history - significant)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Misidentification">Maling Pagtukoy</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="past (past - ordinary) vs. history (history - significant)">nakaraan (past - ordinary) vs. kasaysayan (history - significant)</span>

Slide 20: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong Timeline Writing">Maling Pagsulat ng Timeline</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid mixing up the years when writing a timeline.">Iwasan ang paghahalo ng mga taon sa timeline.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 2020 (Founding) -> 2000 (Clinic) -> 2010 (Road).">Mali: 2020 (Pagtatag) -> 2000 (Klinika) -> 2010 (Daan).</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This does not show the correct flow of time in history.">Hindi nito ipinapakita ang tamang daloy ng panahon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We must start with the oldest year on the left side.">Dapat magsimula sa pinakamatandang taon sa kaliwa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="And end with the most recent year on the right side.">At magtapos sa pinakabagong taon sa kanang bahagi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Correct: 2000 (Founding) -> 2010 (Road) -> 2020 (Clinic).">Tama: 2000 (Pagtatag) -> 2010 (Daan) -> 2020 (Klinika).</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct chronological sequence of our years.">Ito ang wastong pagkakasunod-sunod ng mga taon natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Check the years carefully before drawing your timeline now!">Suriin ang mga taon bago iguhit ang timeline ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Timeline Error: wrong: mixed years -&gt; right: consecutive years">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Timeline Error: mali: naghalong taon -> tama: sunod-sunod na taon</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: Timeline Error: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: mixed years -&gt; right: consecutive years">mali: naghalong taon -> tama: sunod-sunod na taon</span>

Slide 21: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Symbol Misdescription">Maling Paglalarawan ng Simbolo</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid making up meanings for community symbols arbitrarily.">Iwasan ang pag-imbento ng kahulugan ng logo.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Do not say the gear on the logo represents a carriage wheel.">Huwag sabihing ang gear sa logo ay gulong ng karwahe.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="In modern seals, the gear represents factories and industry.">Sa makabagong selyo, ang gear ay para sa industriya.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Verify the history of the place before writing descriptions.">Tiyakin ang kasaysayan ng pook bago maglahad ng tala.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="You can ask the barangay officials inside the barangay hall.">Maaari mong tanungin ang mga barangay officials doon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="They know the real meaning and history of the seal yonder.">Sila ang nakakaalam ng tunay na kahulugan ng selyo.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Accurate records show excellent and high-quality work.">Ang tumpak na tala ay nagpapakita ng mahusay na gawa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Be careful and analytical with every symbol today!">Maging maingat at mapanuri sa bawat simbolo ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Symbol Analysis: gear = industry (factory), NOT carriage wheels">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Simbolo Pagsusuri: gear = industriya (pabrika), HINDI gulong ng karwahe</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Symbol Analysis">Simbolo Pagsusuri</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="gear = industry (factory), NOT carriage wheels">gear = industriya (pabrika), HINDI gulong ng karwahe</span>

Slide 22: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="History of Our Town">Kasaysayan ng Ating Bayan</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Our barangay's history is part of our town's wider history.">Ang kasaysayan ng barangay ay bahagi ng bayan natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Each small place contributes to the history of the province.">Ang bawat maliit na pook ay nag-aambag sa lalawigan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: the history of Koronadal within our province Timog Cotabato.">Halimbawa: ang kasaysayan ng Koronadal sa Timog Cotabato natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Timog Cotabato is known for rich rice fields and beautiful rivers.">Ang Timog Cotabato ay kilala sa saganang palay at magandang ilog.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Our folk songs display this beautiful regional culture.">Ang mga katutubong awitin ay nagpapakita ng kulturang ito.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We take pride in the history of our own local place yonder.">Ipinagmamalaki natin ang kasaysayan ng ating sariling pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This gives us strength and unity in our community life today.">Ito ay nagbibigay sa atin ng lakas at pagkakaisa ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's love our own barangay and province at all times!">Mahalin natin ang ating barangay at lalawigan palagi!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Relationship: barangay -&gt; town -&gt; province">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Ugnayan: barangay -> bayan (town) -> lalawigan (province)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Relationship">Ugnayan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="barangay -&gt; town -&gt; province">barangay -> bayan (town) -> lalawigan (province)</span>

  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Goal of the Week">Layunin ng Linggo</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Recognize one&#x27;s own passions and abilities as part of self-confidence.">Makilala ang sariling hilig at kakayahan bilang bahagi ng tiwala sa sarili.</span>

  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's check how friends help one another in school.">Suriin natin kung paano nagtutulungan ang magkakaibigan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Kiko is very good at math in our classroom today yonder.">Si Kiko ay magaling sa matematika sa aming klase ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="He guided his playmate to compute coins and savings safely.">Tinulungan niya ang kanyang kalaro na magkuwenta ng barya.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Sharing your talent displays excellent moral values in life.">Ang pagbabahagi ng talento ay nagpapakita ng mabuting asal.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="He uses his ability to serve and help his classmates today.">Ginagamit niya ang kanyang kakayahan upang maglingkod.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This makes his teacher and parents very happy and proud.">Ito ay nagpapasaya sa kanyang guro at mga magulang.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Cooperation strengthens the confidence of our entire group.">Ang pagtutulungan ay nagpapatibay ng tiwala ng grupo natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Share your math skills with your seatmate right now!">Ibahagi ang iyong galing sa matematika sa iyong katabi ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Sharing Practice: Kiko -&gt; taught the player to count coins.">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsasanay Pagbabahagi: Kiko -> tinuruan ang kalaro magkuwenta ng barya.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Sharing Practice">Pagsasanay Pagbabahagi</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Kiko -&gt; taught the player to count coins.">Kiko -> tinuruan ang kalaro magkuwenta ng barya.</span>

Slide 11: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Misconception of One&#x27;s Own Greatness">Maling Pag-iisip sa Sariling Galing</span>
  [Current Image: images/gmrc_w1_img2.png]
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid thinking yonder that you have no talent or ability.">Iwasan ang pag-iisip na wala kang kakayahan o talento.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'I have no talent, I cannot do science subjects.'">Mali: 'Wala akong galing, hindi ko kaya ang science.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Every child has a unique strength waiting to be discovered.">Ang bawat bata ay may sariling galing na kailangang tuklasin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Maybe you just need practice and guidance from your teacher.">Maaaring kailangan mo lang ng pagsasanay at gabay ng guro.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Correct: 'I will practice to become good at science today.'">Tama: 'Magsasanay ako upang maging mahusay sa science.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Self-confidence does not surrender at the very first try.">Ang tiwala sa sarili ay hindi sumusuko sa unang subok.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make sure your thoughts are positive in your writing today!">Tiyakin na positibo ang iyong kaisipan sa pagsusulat ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the key to success in everything you perform today!">Ito ang susi sa tagumpay sa lahat ng iyong ginagawa!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Thought Error: wrong: I&#x27;m not good -&gt; right: I will practice to learn">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Kaisipan Error: mali: wala akong galing -> tama: mag-eensayo ako upang matuto</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Thought Error">Kaisipan Error</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: I&#x27;m not good -&gt; right: I will practice to learn">mali: wala akong galing -> tama: mag-eensayo ako upang matuto</span>

Slide 12: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="False Boasting of Talent">Maling Pagyayabang ng Talento</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid boasting or showing off when you are already skilled.">Iwasan ang pagmamayabang kapag ikaw ay mahusay na.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'I am better than all of you at reading books yonder!'">Mali: 'Mas magaling ako sa inyong lahat sa pagbasa!'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Boasting does not display true and healthy self-confidence.">Ang pagyayabang ay hindi nagpapakita ng tiwala sa sarili.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It displays lack of humility and respect for your classmates.">Ito ay nagpapakita ng kawalan ng kababaang-loob sa kapwa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The truly confident student serves others quietly in school.">Ang tunay na may tiwala ay tahimik na naglilingkod.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="He helps those who struggle without making them feel bad.">Tinutulungan niya ang mga nahihirapan nang walang yabang.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct moral value taught in our GMRC class.">Ito ang wastong asal na itinuturo sa ating GMRC.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Be humble at all times and share your talents with others!">Maging mababa ang loob at palaging magbahagi ng biyaya!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Arrogant Error: wrong: show off in class -&gt; right: help with humility">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Yabang Error: mali: magyabang sa klase -> tama: tumulong nang may kababaang-loob</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Arrogant Error">Yabang Error</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: show off in class -&gt; right: help with humility">mali: magyabang sa klase -> tama: tumulong nang may kababaang-loob</span>

Slide 13: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The Self-Evaluation">Ang Pagtatasa sa Sariling Galing</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's check our own progress and development every day.">Suriin natin ang ating sariling pag-unlad araw-araw.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make a written list of your hobbies and abilities today.">Gumawa ng listahan ng iyong mga hilig at kakayahan ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Write down what practice routines you are doing at home.">Isulat kung anong mga pagsasanay ang iyong ginagawa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="E.g., practicing refining drawings in the afternoon hours.">E.g., nag-eensayo ng pagpapakinis ng guhit sa hapon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Self-assessment displays our personal discipline yonder.">Ang pagtatasa sa sarili ay nagpapakita ng disiplina natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We find out where we still need to study and put in effort.">Nalalaman natin kung saan pa natin kailangang mag-aral.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Ask for guidance from your teacher or parents in this task.">Humingi ng tulong sa guro o magulang para sa pagsusuri.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Continue developing your own special talents in the community!">Ipagpatuloy ang pag-unlad ng iyong sariling talento ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Assessment: Self-assessment: What am I good at? How can I improve it?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagtatasa: Suriin ang sarili: Ano ang aking galing? Paano ko ito mapapahusay?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Assessment">Pagtatasa</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Self-assessment: What am I good at? How can I improve it?">Suriin ang sarili: Ano ang aking galing? Paano ko ito mapapahusay?</span>

Slide 0: Understanding Area
  Text: Let's learn how to measure the flat space covered by a shape. We call this space the area of the shape. To measure it, we cover the surface completely with smaller, identical units. In math, we express this as: Area = covered surface space. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces. We must make sure that every tile lies flat and touches the edges of the neighboring tiles. Counting each unit one by one is simple, but multiplication makes the process much faster. The total area is directly related to the length and width of the covering grid. Can you look at your desk and imagine covering it with square papers?
  Example: Example 1: Review standard details: Area = covered surface space.

Slide 1: The Concept of Square Tiles
  Text: A square tile is a shape with four equal sides. It is the perfect unit for measuring area because squares fit together side-by-side without leaving gaps. In math, we express this as: 1 tile = 1 unit of area. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces. We must make sure that every tile lies flat and touches the edges of the neighboring tiles. Counting each unit one by one is simple, but multiplication makes the process much faster. The total area is directly related to the length and width of the covering grid. How does using the same size of square tiles help us get an accurate measurement?
  Example: Example 2: Review standard details: 1 tile = 1 unit of area.

Slide 2: Covering Surfaces Perfectly
  Text: When we cover a shape to find its area, we must make sure there are no gaps or overlaps. Every square tile must touch the edge of the next tile. In math, we express this as: Total Area = Sum of all tiles. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces. We must make sure that every tile lies flat and touches the edges of the neighboring tiles. Counting each unit one by one is simple, but multiplication makes the process much faster. The total area is directly related to the length and width of the covering grid. What would happen to our area count if some tiles overlapped each other?
  Example: Example 3: Review standard details: Total Area = Sum of all tiles.

Slide 3: Rows and Columns in a Grid
  Text: To organize our tiles, we arrange them in neat rows that go across and columns that go down. This arrangement forms a grid pattern on the surface. In math, we express this as: Grid = Rows x Columns. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces. We must make sure that every tile lies flat and touches the edges of the neighboring tiles. Counting each unit one by one is simple, but multiplication makes the process much faster. The total area is directly related to the length and width of the covering grid. Multiplying rows by columns gives the exact number of squares without counting them individually. Can you count the number of rows and columns on a tiled floor?
  Example: Example 4: Review standard details: Grid = Rows x Columns.

Slide 4: Counting Tiles by Rows
  [Current Image: images/math_w1_img1.png]
  Text: We can find the total area of a grid by adding the tiles in each row. If there are 4 rows with 4 tiles each, we add 4 four times. In math, we express this as: Total = 4 + 4 + 4 + 4 = 16. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces. We must make sure that every tile lies flat and touches the edges of the neighboring tiles. Counting each unit one by one is simple, but multiplication makes the process much faster. The total area is directly related to the length and width of the covering grid. Why is adding by rows faster than counting each tile one by one?
  Example: Example 5: Review standard details: Total = 4 + 4 + 4 + 4 = 16.

Slide 5: Counting Tiles by Columns
  Text: Just like adding by rows, we can also count tiles by columns. If we have 4 columns of 5 tiles, we add 5 four times to get the area. In math, we express this as: Total = 5 + 5 + 5 + 5 = 20. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces.
