Slide 22: Common Error: Overlapping Tiles
  Text: A common mistake when measuring area is letting the tiles overlap. This makes our count too small because some space is covered twice by the same tiles. Slide 23: Common Error: Leaving Gaps
  Text: Another mistake is leaving gaps between tiles. Gaps make our area measurement inaccurate because we are not counting the empty space between the tiles. In math, we express this as: Gaps = Empty spaces in measurement. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces. We must make sure that every tile lies flat and touches the edges of the neighboring tiles. Counting each unit one by one is simple, but multiplication makes the process much faster. The total area is directly related to the length and width of the covering grid. Multiplying rows by columns gives the exact number of squares without counting them individually. Why must tiles touch edge-to-edge to give a true area measurement?
  Example: Example 24: Review standard details: Gaps = Empty spaces in measurement.

Slide 24: Review of Area Concepts
  Text: Let's summarize what we learned. Area measures covered flat space. We cover shapes with square tiles, count them, or use the multiplication formula: Area equals Length times Width. In math, we express this as: Area = space covered on a flat surface. Let's learn and master this key mathematical concept. A square tile has equal sides, which makes it the standard base for measuring flat spaces. We must make sure that every tile lies flat and touches the edges of the neighboring tiles. Counting each unit one by one is simple, but multiplication makes the process much faster. The total area is directly related to the length and width of the covering grid. How will you explain the concept of area to a friend today?
  Example: Example 25: Review standard details: Area = space covered on a flat surface.

Slide 23: Common Error: Concluding Too Early
  Text: Do not draw scientific conclusions from a single trial. Repeat experiments for accuracy. For instance, consider the example of Incorrect: Testing one seed and concluding that all seeds grow in three days. For instance, consider the example of Correct: Testing twenty seeds and calculating the average germination rate. To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. Slide 1: Spotting Ending Sounds (CVCC)
  Text: Look at your hand. Let's say it slowly: h-a-n-d. Hear how the letters 'n' and 'd' blend at the end? This is a CVCC word: Consonant-Vowel-Consonant-Consonant. It ends with two consonants that make a blended sound. We call these ending consonant blends in phonics. They are very common in the words we use every day. Let's learn how to spot and spell them correctly. We will search for CVCC words in our environment today! For instance, consider the example of Word Pattern: C = Consonant, V = Vowel, C = Consonant, C = Consonant. To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems.
  Example: Word Pattern: C = Consonant, V = Vowel, C = Consonant, C = Consonant.
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 2: Phonics Hunt: In the Tent
  Text: Imagine we are camping under the dark night sky. We set up a strong green tent on the ground. Look at the word 'tent'. It ends with 'nt'. The letters 'n' and 't' blend together smoothly. Let's practice saying the word 'tent' three times. Feel the blend of 'n' and 't' on your tongue. We spell it as t - e - n - t. It is a perfect example of a CVCC word! To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.

For instance, consider the example of Spelling: d - e - s - k and h - u - n - t To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Spelling: d - e - s - k  and  h - u - n - t
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 8: Grammar: Pointing to Things
  Text: When we observe nature, we need to point to things. We use special words called demonstrative pronouns. These pronouns tell us if an object is near or far. They also tell us if there is one object or many. The four pronouns are: this, that, these, and those. They help make our descriptions clear and specific. Let's learn how to use them like real scientists. We will practice pointing to objects in our room! For instance, consider the example of Focus Pronouns: This, That, These, Those To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Focus Pronouns: This, That, These, Those
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 9: Near Us: This and These
  Text: Look at the pencil you are holding in your hand. You can say: 'This is my pencil.' (one object). Now look at the fingers on your own hand. You can say: 'These are my fingers.' (many objects). We use 'this' for a single object near us. We use 'these' for multiple objects close to us. Both words show that the objects are within reach. Try touching a book and saying: 'This is my book.' For instance, consider the example of Near Examples: This pencil (1 near), These rocks (many near). To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems.
  Example: Near Examples: This pencil (1 near), These rocks (many near).
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 10: Far From Us: That and Those
  Text: Look out the window at the distant sky. You see a bird and say: 'That is a bird.' (one far). You see clouds and say: 'Those are clouds.' (many far). We use 'that' for a single object far away. We use 'those' for multiple objects far away. These words show that the objects are out of reach. Point to a distant tree and say: 'That is a tree.' Point to stars and say: 'Those are stars.' For instance, consider the example of Far Examples: That star (1 far), Those mountains (many far). To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems.
  Example: Far Examples: That star (1 far), Those mountains (many far).
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 11: Sentence Engine: Declarative Sentences
  [Current Image: images/english_w1_img2.png]
  Text: A telling sentence is like a small train. It makes a statement to tell a fact or observation. We call this a declarative sentence in grammar. It must always start with a capital letter. It must always end with a period punctuation mark. It has a subject (who or what the sentence is about). It has a predicate (what the subject is or does). Let's build a declarative sentence together! For instance, consider the example of Rule: Always start with a capital letter and end with a period. To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Rule: Always start with a capital letter and end with a period.
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 12: Declarative: Spotting the Parts
  Text: Let's look at: 'Matteo rides a calesa.' 'Matteo' is the subject because he is the person. 'rides a calesa' is the predicate (the action). Together, they tell us a complete factual statement. Notice the capital 'M' at the beginning of the sentence. Notice the period at the end of the sentence. Without a subject and predicate, a sentence is incomplete. Always check both parts when you write in your journal! To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Subject: Matteo
  Example: Predicate: rides a calesa
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 13: Story Time: The Calesa Ride
  Text: Let's read a short story about Matteo's day: 'Matteo sits inside a wooden calesa on the street. The fast horse walks down the paved town road. Matteo smiles at the colorful houses along the way. He observes the busy community starting their morning.' This story is made of declarative sentences. They tell us exactly what Matteo does and sees. Read it aloud to practice your reading flow! For instance, consider the example of Reading Task: Read the story aloud to practice your spelling words! To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Reading Task: Read the story aloud to practice your spelling words!
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 14: Characters: Who is in the Story?
  Text: Every story has characters that make it interesting. Characters are the people, animals, or creatures. They perform actions and speak words in the plot. In our story, the characters are Matteo and the horse. Understanding characters helps us connect with the story. We can think about how they feel and what they want. Who is your favorite character in the calesa story? Write down their names on your paper! For instance, consider the example of Key Concept: Characters = Who To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Key Concept: Characters = Who
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 15: Setting: Where and When?
  Text: The setting is where and when the story takes place. It provides the background environment for the characters. In our story, the setting is a historic town street. The time of the story is a sunny morning. Knowing the setting helps us picture the events. It is like looking at a photograph of the scene. Where does your favorite daily activity take place? That place is the setting of your own daily story! For instance, consider the example of Key Concept: Setting = Where and When To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Key Concept: Setting = Where and When
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 16: Plot: What Happens?
  Text: The plot is the sequence of events in a story. It tells us what happens first, next, and last. First, Matteo gets inside the wooden calesa. Next, the horse walks down the paved town street. Finally, Matteo smiles at the colorful houses. A clear plot makes stories easy to understand. It helps us follow the character's journey. Can you retell the plot of Matteo's ride in order? For instance, consider the example of Key Concept: Plot = What happens (First, Next, Then) To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Key Concept: Plot = What happens (First, Next, Then)
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 17: Observing Local Transport
  Text: In our local community, we observe unique transport. A calesa is a carriage drawn by a horse on land. It has two large wheels and a wooden passenger cabin. A banca is a small outrigger boat used on water. It helps fishermen travel across rivers and seas. Both transport types are important to our heritage. They are perfect topics for our declarative sentences. Let's write a sentence about a banca today! To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Land Transport: calesa
  Example: Water Transport: banca
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 18: Nature Connections: The Wet Sand
  [Current Image: images/english_w1_img3.png]
  Text: Let's walk down to the riverbank to explore. We observe wet sand near the flowing water. Let's write: 'This sand is wet and cold.' 'Sand' is a CVCC spelling word ending in 'nd'. 'This' points to the sand right under our feet. This sentence is a telling (declarative) sentence. It starts with a capital letter and ends with a period. We are using English to describe our science observations! For instance, consider the example of Observation: Pointing to sand near your feet: 'This is wet sand.' To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.

Slide 19: Science Connection: The Pink Fish
  Text: Look at the clear water in the stream. We point to a swimming fish: 'That is a pink fish.' 'Pink' is a CVCC word ending in the blend 'nk'. 'That' points to the fish swimming far from us. This is a factual observation about the natural world. It uses our senses to collect details about animals. Always look closely at the color of fish scales. What other scale colors can you observe in the water? For instance, consider the example of Observation: Pointing to fish in the pond: 'That is a pink fish.' To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems.
  Example: Observation: Pointing to fish in the pond: 'That is a pink fish.'
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 20: Guided Practice: Spotting CVCC Words
  Text: Let's play a game to spot CVCC words. Read this: 'The child sat at the wooden desk.' Which word ends with a double consonant blend? Yes, the word is 'desk'! It ends with 'sk'. The other words do not follow the CVCC pattern. Spelling 'desk' correctly requires the letters d-e-s-k. Can you find another CVCC word in your classroom? Look at the lamp or the window frame! For instance, consider the example of Check: d - e - s - k ends with the consonants s and k. To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Check: d - e - s - k ends with the consonants s and k.
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 21: Guided Practice: Near or Far?
  Text: Let's practice choosing the correct pronoun. If you are holding a flower, what do you say? 'A. This is a flower.' or 'B. That is a flower.'? Since the flower is in your hand, choose A! If a bird is high on a tree branch, you say: 'That is a bird on the branch.' Use 'this' for near, and 'that' for far away. It is as simple as measuring distance with your eyes! For instance, consider the example of Rule of Thumb: If you can touch it, use 'this' or 'these'. To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems.
  Example: Rule of Thumb: If you can touch it, use 'this' or 'these'.
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 22: Guided Practice: Capital and Period
  Text: Let's check the rules for telling sentences. Look at: 'the banca floats in the river' What is missing from this declarative sentence? It must start with a capital 'T' for 'The'. It must end with a period at the end of 'river'. Let's write it correctly: 'The banca floats in the river.' Now it has a subject and a predicate. It is a complete and correct sentence! To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation. Every example we observe helps us connect theoretical knowledge with practical real-world applications.
  Example: Corrected: 'The banca floats in the river.'
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 23: Common Error: Mixing Near and Far
  Text: A common mistake is using 'this' for far objects. If a star is shining in the sky, do not say: 'This is a bright star.' (It is too far to touch!). Instead, say: 'That is a bright star.' If the books are far on the shelf, do not say: 'These are my books.' (They are out of reach!). Instead, say: 'Those are my books.' Always check the distance before you choose the pronoun! For instance, consider the example of Correction: 'Those clouds look soft.' To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives. By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems. It is important to practice regularly and discuss these ideas with your peers and teachers to build a strong foundation.
  Example: Correction: 'Those clouds look soft.'
  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 24: Summary of Week 1
  Text: Congratulations! You completed all the slides for Week 1. Let's review the main language tools we mastered. We learned to decode CVCC words like tent, lamp, and desk. We learned to point using this, that, these, and those. We learned to write declarative sentences with periods. We learned to identify story characters, settings, and plots. We connected our English lessons to science observations. You are now ready to take the quiz and challenges! By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills and learn to solve complex problems.

  Example: HOTS Challenge: How would you apply this linguistic pattern to create a complex sentence?

Slide 4: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Comparing Writing">Pagkukumpara sa Pagsulat</span>
  [Current Image: images/filipino_w1_img1.png]
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's compare the two types of nouns side by side.">Pagkumparahin natin ang dalawang uri ng pangngalan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The common noun is 'country', the proper is 'Philippines'.">Ang pambalana ay 'bansa', ang pantangi ay 'Pilipinas'.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The common noun is 'province', the proper is 'Timog Cotabato'.">Ang pambalana ay 'lalawigan', ang pantangi ay 'Timog Cotabato'.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The common noun is 'school', the proper is 'Koronadal School'.">Ang pambalana ay 'paaralan', ang pantangi ay 'Paaralang Koronadal'.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Did you notice the use of the capital letter?">Napansin mo ba ang paggamit ng malaking titik?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Proper nouns have their own identity in language.">Ang pantangi ay may sariling pagkakakilanlan sa wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Common nouns remain general in their written form.">Ang pambalana ay nananatiling pangkalahatan ang anyo.</span> <span Slide 5: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The Home and Community">Ang Tahanan at Komunidad</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Our home is an important place for all of us.">Ang ating tahanan ay isang mahalagang pook sa atin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The common noun for it is 'home' or 'house'.">Ang pambalana para rito ay 'tahanan' o 'bahay'.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The proper noun is your own specific address today.">Ang pantangi naman ay ang iyong sariling address ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: '123 Rizal Street' is a proper noun.">Halimbawa: '123 Kalye Rizal' ay isang pangngalang pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Outside the house, we can see the barangay hall.">Sa labas ng bahay, makikita natin ang barangay hall.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The term 'barangay hall' is a common noun in our language.">Ang 'barangay hall' ay pambalana sa ating wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="But 'Barangay San Juan Hall' is a proper noun already.">Ngunit ang 'Barangay San Juan Hall' ay pantangi na.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Look at your surroundings and list down places!">Masdan ang iyong paligid at maglista ng pook!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Community: home (common) -&gt;   Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The school is a place where we study together.">Ang paaralan ay pook kung saan tayo nag-aaral.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The word 'school' is a general common noun.">Ang 'paaralan' ay pangkalahatang pangngalang pambalana.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We have different rooms inside the school building.">Mayroon tayong iba't ibang silid sa loob nito.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There is the classroom, library, office, and restroom.">May silid-aralan, aklatan, opisina, at palikuran.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="All of these rooms are common nouns in language.">Ang lahat ng silid na ito ay pambalana sa wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="But the specific name of your school is a proper noun.">Ngunit ang pangalan ng iyong eskwelahan ay pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: 'Polomolok Elementary School' is proper.">Halimbawa: 'Paaralang Elementarya ng Polomolok' ay pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Always write it using capital letters!">Lagi itong isulat gamit ang malalaking titik!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of school: library (library - Slide 13: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Sentence Analysis">Pagsusuri sa Pangungusap</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's analyze the place nouns in sentences.">Suriin natin ang mga pook sa pangungusap.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Statement: 'We went to a big school.'">Pahayag: 'Pumunta kami sa isang malaking paaralan.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place here is 'school' which is a common noun.">Ang pook dito ay 'paaralan' na isang pambalana.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Another statement: 'We are studying in Koronadal.'">Isa pang pahayag: 'Kami ay nag-aaral sa Koronadal.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place here is 'Koronadal' which is a proper noun.">Ang pook dito ay 'Koronadal' na isang pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is the specific name of a city in Timog Cotabato.">Ito ay tiyak na ngalan ng lungsod sa Timog Cotabato.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="So it starts with the capital letter C.">Kaya nagsisimula ito sa malaking titik na C.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Is it easy to identify these places in sentences?">Madali lang bang matukoy ang mga pook na ito?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Analysis: school (common noun) vs. Koronadal (proper noun)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsusuri: paaralan (common noun) vs. Koronadal (proper noun)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How Slide 14: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Capitalization Rule">Panuntunan sa Malaking Titik</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Why is the capital letter important for proper nouns?">Bakit mahalaga ang malaking titik sa pantangi?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It indicates the specific and unique name of a place.">Ito ay nagpapakita ng tiyak na ngalan ng pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="If we write 'pilipinas' in lowercase, it is wrong.">Kung isusulat natin ang 'pilipinas', ito ay mali.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It must be written as 'Pilipinas' with a capital P.">Dapat itong isulat na 'Pilipinas' na may malaking P.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Likewise for 'lawa ng sebu', it must be 'Lawa ng Sebu'.">Gayundin sa 'lawa ng sebu', dapat ay 'Lawa ng Sebu'.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Capital letter L and capital letter S are both required.">Malaki ang titik L at malaki rin ang titik S.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct spelling and grammar in our language.">Ito ang wastong bantas at baybay sa ating wika.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Practice writing this correctly every single day!">Sanayin ang sarili sa pagsulat nito araw-araw!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Proper Writing: wrong: lake sebu -&gt;   Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's check the spelling of the following places.">Suriin natin ang pagsulat ng mga sumusunod na pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Statement: 'He lives in barangay san Juan.'">Pahayag: 'Nakatira siya sa barangay san Juan.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Is there a mistake in writing this place name?">Mayroon bang pagkakamali sa pagsulat ng pook na ito?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Yes, 'barangay san Juan' should be a proper noun.">Oo, ang 'barangay san Juan' ay dapat maging pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It must be written as 'Barangay San Juan' with capitals.">Dapat itong isulat na 'Barangay San Juan' na malaki.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Capital B, capital S, and capital J are all needed.">Malaki ang titik B, malaki ang S, at malaki ang J.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct way to write our barangay name.">Ito ang tamang paraan ng pagsulat ng ating barangay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Always be careful with capital letters in your writing!">Palaging maging maingat sa malalaking titik sa pagsulat!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Training: wrong: barangay san juan -&gt; Slide 20: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Letter Misuse">Maling Paggamit ng Titik</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid writing common nouns with capital letters.">Iwasan ang pagsusulat ng pambalana sa malaking titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'We went to a Hospital.' (common noun capitalized)">Mali: 'Pumunta kami sa isang Ospital.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The word 'hospital' is just a common noun here.">Ang 'ospital' ay pambalana lamang sa pangungusap.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="So it should be written with a lowercase letter o.">Kaya dapat itong isulat sa maliit na titik o.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Correct: 'We went to a hospital.' (lowercase o)">Tama: 'Pumunta kami sa isang ospital.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Do not capitalize the letter if it is not specific.">Huwag lakihan ang titik kung hindi ito tiyak.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is a common mistake made by young learners.">Ito ay isang karaniwang pagkakamali ng mga bata.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make sure your letters are correct in your writing now!">Tiyakin na tama ang iyong mga titik sa pagsulat ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Wrong letter: wrong: Hospital -&gt; right: hospital">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Maling Titik: mali: Ospital -> tama: ospital</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>

Slide 21: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Identifying Categories">Pagkilala sa mga Kategorya</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Do not confuse people or things with places.">Huwag ipagpalit ang tao o bagay sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The 'teacher' is a person; the 'school' is a place.">Ang 'guro' ay tao; ang 'paaralan' ay pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The 'book' is a thing; the 'library' is a place.">Ang 'aklat' ay bagay; ang 'aklatan' ay pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The 'doctor' is a person; the 'hospital' is a place.">Ang 'doktor' ay tao; ang 'ospital' ay pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Analyze carefully what the word is referring to.">Suriin nang mabuti kung ano ang tinutukoy ng salita.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Is it a location, or an object, or a person?">Ito ba ay isang lugar o kagamitan o tao?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Classifying into categories is an important skill.">Ang pag-uri sa kategorya ay mahalagang kasanayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This will help in understanding the meaning of words!">Makatutulong ito sa pag-unawa ng kahulugan ng salita!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Category: book (thing) vs. library (place)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Kategorya: aklat (bagay) vs. aklatan (pook - place)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>

Slide 22: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Why Does Location Matter?">Bakit Mahalaga ang Pook?</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Places provide the setting for our stories.">Ang mga pook ay nagbibigay ng setting sa kwento.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is where all important events take place.">Dito nagaganap ang lahat ng mahahalagang pangyayari.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="In writing stories, we need to specify the place.">Sa pagsulat ng kwento, kailangan natin ang pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Specifying the place gives clarity to the reader.">Ang pagtukoy sa pook ay nagbibigay-linaw sa mambabasa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We can use either common or proper nouns.">Maaari nating gamitin ang pambalana o pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This depends on whether we want to be specific or not.">Depende ito kung nais nating maging tiyak o hindi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Use your knowledge to write a short story!">Gamitin ang iyong kaalaman upang sumulat ng kwento!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Share it with your teacher and classmates today!">Ibahagi ito sa iyong guro at mga kamag-aral ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Importance: Place answers the question: Where? (Where?)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Kahalagahan: Ang pook ay sumasagot sa tanong na: Saan? (Where?)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>

Slide 23: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Area Writing Guide">Gabay sa Pagsusulat ng Pook</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Here is a quick guide to writing places correctly.">Narito ang mabilis na gabay sa pagsusulat ng pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="First, determine if it is common or proper.">Una, alamin kung ito ay pambalana o pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Second, if it is proper, capitalize the first letter.">Pangalawa, kung ito ay pantangi, lakihan ang titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Third, if common, use lowercase first letters.">Pangatlo, kung pambalana, gamitin ang maliit na titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Fourth, make sure of the correct spelling of words.">Pang-apat, tiyakin ang tamang baybay ng mga salita.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: 'Lungsod ng San Pablo' has capital L and S.">Halimbawa: 'Lungsod ng San Pablo' ay may malaking L at S.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The connecting word 'ng' remains in lowercase.">Ang salitang 'ng' ay nananatiling maliit ang titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Follow this guide in your practice exercises today!">Sundan ang gabay na ito sa iyong mga pagsasanay ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of guide: Special -&gt; Upper case. Symbol -&gt; Lower case.">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Gabay: Pantangi -> Malaking titik. Pambalana -> Maliit na titik.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="guide">Gabay</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Special -&gt; Upper case. Symbol -&gt; Lower case.">Pantangi -> Malaking titik. Pambalana -> Maliit na titik.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="HOTS Challenge">HOTS Hamon</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span>

Slide 1: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What is History?">Ano ang Kasaysayan?</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="History is not just simply old stories from the past.">Ang kasaysayan ay hindi lamang basta lumang kwento.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is the study of meaningful past events in lives.">Ito ay pag-aaral ng may-saysay na nakaraang yugto.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There are four important elements of history we study today.">May apat na mahahalagang elemento ang kasaysayan ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="These are the people, place, time, and the event itself.">Ito ang tao, lugar, panahon, at ang pangyayari.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It answers who, where, when, and what happened yonder.">Sinasagot nito ang sino, saan, class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This helps us understand our present life in communities.">Nakatutulong ito sa pag-unawa ng ating kasalukuyan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" Slide 6: Primary Sources: Artifacts
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How do we know the history of our local community?">Paano natin nalalaman ang kasaysayan ng komunidad?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" Slide 14: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Local Songs and Dances">Mga Lokal na Awitin at Sayaw</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Local folk songs describe the daily way of life of people.">Ang mga lokal na awitin ay naglalarawan ng buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" Slide 15: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Guided Practice: The Review">Guided Practice: Ang Pagsusuri</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's analyze a short story of our local history.">Suriin natin ang isang kwento ng ating kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Read: 'Barangay San Jose was founded in the year 1950.'">Basahin: 'Itinatag ang Barangay San Jose noong 1950.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Identify the place mentioned in our statement yonder.">Tukuyin ang pook na binanggit sa ating pahayag.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place is 'Barangay San Jose' which is proper.">Ang pook ay 'Barangay San Jose' na isang pantangi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Identify the time period mentioned in our statement.">Tukuyin ang panahon na binanggit sa ating pahayag.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The time is 'in 1950' which is a specific year.">Ang panahon ay 'noong 1950' na isang tiyak na taon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The founding is the event that has deep historical meaning.">Ang pagtatag ay ang pangyayaring may malalim na saysay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Did you find all three elements in your analysis today?">Nahanap mo ba ang tatlong elemento sa pagsusuri?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Analysis: Place -&gt; Barangay San Jose, Period -&gt; 1950, Event -&gt; Establishment">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsusuri: Pook -> Barangay San Jose, Panahon -> 1950, Pangyayari -> Pagtatag</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Analysis">Pagsusuri</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Place -&gt; Barangay San Jose, Period -&gt; 1950, Event -&gt; Establishment">Pook -> Barangay San Jose, Panahon -> 1950, Pangyayari -> Pagtatag</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="HOTS Challenge">HOTS Hamon</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span>

Slide 16: Guided Practice: Primary vs Secondary
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's check the following sources of historical data.">Suriin natin ang mga sumusunod na batayan ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="If you find an old coin dated with the year 1900,">Kung nakakita ka ng lumang barya na may taong 1900,</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="this is a primary source (artifact) for the place.">ito ay isang primaryang batayan (artifact) sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="If you read the book 'History of Timog Cotabato' in class,">Kung binabasa mo ang aklat na 'Kasaysayan ng Timog Cotabato',</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="this is a secondary source in our history lesson today.">ito ay isang sekondaryang batayan sa ating aralin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The book was written by a researcher after studying coins.">Ang aklat ay isinulat ng mananaliksik pagkatapos.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Both sources of data are valuable for historical study.">Parehong mahalaga ang dalawang batayan sa kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Which would you prefer to examine: the coin or the book?">Alin ang mas nais mong suriin: barya o aklat?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Basis: old coin -&gt; primary, textbook -&gt; secondary">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Batayan: lumang barya -> primary, textbook -> secondary</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="By studying this topic, students can develop critical thinking skills.">Sa pamamagitan ng pag-aaral ng paksang ito, ang mga mag-aaral ay maaaring bumuo ng mga kasanayan sa kritikal na pag-iisip.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Basis">Batayan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="old coin -&gt; primary, textbook -&gt; secondary">lumang barya -> primary, textbook -> secondary</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="HOTS Challenge">HOTS Hamon</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span>

Slide 17: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Guided Practice: Area Timeline">Guided Practice: Timeline ng Pook</span>

Slide 18: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Guided Practice: Logo Analysis">Guided Practice: Pagsusuri ng Logo</span>
  [Current Image: images/makabansa_w1_img3.png]
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's analyze the logo of a barangay near our school.">Suriin natin ang logo ng isang barangay sa tabi natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="There is a drawing of three fish and a net in the middle.">May guhit ng tatlong isda at lambat sa gitna nito.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="What is the meaning of the fish on this local logo?">Ano ang ibig sabihin ng mga isda sa logo ng pook?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It shows that fishing is the main source of livelihood there.">Ipinapakita nito na pangingisda ang kabuhayan doon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The place is near a lake or sea, hence the fish symbol.">Ang pook ay malapit sa lawa o dagat kaya may isda.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This expresses the story of the people's way of life.">Ito ay naglalahad ng kwento ng pamumuhay ng tao.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is not just decoration; it holds a deep meaning yonder.">Ito ay hindi lamang palamuti; may malalim na saysay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Draw the logo of your own barangay on a clean sheet of paper!">Iguhit ang logo ng iyong barangay sa isang malinis na papel!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Logo Analysis: fish and nets -&gt; fishing livelihood">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Pagsusuri ng Logo: isda at lambat -> kabuhayan sa pangingisda (fishing)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>

Slide 19: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Misidentifying the Past">Maling Pagtukoy sa Nakaraan</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid treating ordinary past events as historical events.">Iwasan ang pagtrato sa ordinaryong bagay bilang kasaysayan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'My eating of bread yesterday is part of history.'">Mali: 'Ang pagkain ko ng tinapay kahapon ay kasaysayan.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It is just the past, but has no major significance to the town.">Ito ay nakaraan lamang, ngunit walang saysay sa pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="History must have a major and lasting impact on the community.">Ang kasaysayan ay dapat may malaking epekto sa lahat.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: the construction of the first bridge over the river.">Halimbawa: ang pagpapatayo ng unang tulay sa ilog.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This changed transport for the entire local community.">Ito ay binago ang transportasyon ng buong komunidad.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make sure the event is significant in your history logs!">Tiyakin na makabuluhan ang pangyayari sa iyong logs!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the true meaning of history in our social studies!">Ito ang totoong kahulugan ng kasaysayan sa atin!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Misidentification: past (past - ordinary) vs. history (history - significant)">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Maling Pagtukoy: nakaraan (past - ordinary) vs. kasaysayan (history - significant)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Misidentification">Maling Pagtukoy</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="past (past - ordinary) vs. history (history - significant)">nakaraan (past - ordinary) vs. kasaysayan (history - significant)</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="HOTS Challenge">HOTS Hamon</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span>

Slide 20: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong Timeline Writing">Maling Pagsulat ng Timeline</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid mixing up the years when writing a timeline.">Iwasan ang paghahalo ng mga taon sa timeline.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 2020 (Founding) -> 2000 (Clinic) -> 2010 (Road).">Mali: 2020 (Pagtatag) -> 2000 (Klinika) -> 2010 (Daan).</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This does not show the correct flow of time in history.">Hindi nito ipinapakita ang tamang daloy ng panahon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We must start with the oldest year on the left side.">Dapat magsimula sa pinakamatandang taon sa kaliwa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="And end with the most recent year on the right side.">At magtapos sa pinakabagong taon sa kanang bahagi.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Correct: 2000 (Founding) -> 2010 (Road) -> 2020 (Clinic).">Tama: 2000 (Pagtatag) -> 2010 (Daan) -> 2020 (Klinika).</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct chronological sequence of our years.">Ito ang wastong pagkakasunod-sunod ng mga taon natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Check the years carefully before drawing your timeline now!">Suriin ang mga taon bago iguhit ang timeline ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Timeline Error: wrong: mixed years -&gt; right: consecutive years">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Timeline Error: mali: naghalong taon -> tama: sunod-sunod na taon</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: Timeline Error: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: mixed years -&gt; right: consecutive years">mali: naghalong taon -> tama: sunod-sunod na taon</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="HOTS Challenge">HOTS Hamon</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span>

Slide 21: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Symbol Misdescription">Maling Paglalarawan ng Simbolo</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid making up meanings for community symbols arbitrarily.">Iwasan ang pag-imbento ng kahulugan ng logo.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Do not say the gear on the logo represents a carriage wheel.">Huwag sabihing ang gear sa logo ay gulong ng karwahe.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="In modern seals, the gear represents factories and industry.">Sa makabagong selyo, ang gear ay para sa industriya.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Verify the history of the place before writing descriptions.">Tiyakin ang kasaysayan ng pook bago maglahad ng tala.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="You can ask the barangay officials inside the barangay hall.">Maaari mong tanungin ang mga barangay officials doon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="They know the real meaning and history of the seal yonder.">Sila ang nakakaalam ng tunay na kahulugan ng selyo.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Accurate records show excellent and high-quality work.">Ang tumpak na tala ay nagpapakita ng mahusay na gawa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Be careful and analytical with every symbol today!">Maging maingat at mapanuri sa bawat simbolo ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Symbol Analysis: gear = industry (factory), NOT carriage wheels">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Simbolo Pagsusuri: gear = industriya (pabrika), HINDI gulong ng karwahe</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Symbol Analysis">Simbolo Pagsusuri</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="gear = industry (factory), NOT carriage wheels">gear = industriya (pabrika), HINDI gulong ng karwahe</span>

Slide 22: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="History of Our Town">Kasaysayan ng Ating Bayan</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Our barangay's history is part of our town's wider history.">Ang kasaysayan ng barangay ay bahagi ng bayan natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Each small place contributes to the history of the province.">Ang bawat maliit na pook ay nag-aambag sa lalawigan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Example: the history of Koronadal within our province Timog Cotabato.">Halimbawa: ang kasaysayan ng Koronadal sa Timog Cotabato natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Timog Cotabato is known for rich rice fields and beautiful rivers.">Ang Timog Cotabato ay kilala sa saganang palay at magandang ilog.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Our folk songs display this beautiful regional culture.">Ang mga katutubong awitin ay nagpapakita ng kulturang ito.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We take pride in the history of our own local place yonder.">Ipinagmamalaki natin ang kasaysayan ng ating sariling pook.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This gives us strength and unity in our community life today.">Ito ay nagbibigay sa atin ng lakas at pagkakaisa ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's love our own barangay and province at all times!">Mahalin natin ang ating barangay at lalawigan palagi!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Relationship: barangay -&gt; town -&gt; province">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Ugnayan: barangay -> bayan (town) -> lalawigan (province)</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Relationship">Ugnayan</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="barangay -&gt; town -&gt; province">barangay -> bayan (town) -> lalawigan (province)</span>

Slide 8: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Guided Practice: Identifying Passion">Guided Practice: Pagtukoy sa Hilig</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's practice identifying hobbies and talents today.">Magsanay tayo sa pagtukoy ng hilig at kakayahan ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Analyze: 'Matteo loves drawing pictures of flying birds.'">Suriin: 'Gustong-gusto ni Matteo ang gumuhit ng ibon.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Drawing birds is his personal interest or hobby in life.">Ang pagguhit ng ibon ay ang kanyang 'hilig' sa buhay.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Because he practices frequently in his school notebook,">Dahil madalas siyang mag-ensayo sa kanyang notebook,</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="he became very skilled at drawing different animals yonder.">siya ay naging napakahusay mag-drawing ng mga hayop.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Being good at drawing is his developed talent or ability.">Ang pagiging mahusay mag-drawing ay ang kanyang kakayahan.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Were you able to distinguish hobby and ability today?">Nagawa mo bang pag-ibahin ang hilig at kakayahan ngayon?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This will help in understanding your own personal talents!">Ito ay makatutulong sa pag-unawa ng iyong sariling galing!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Analysis: Like (Inclination) -&gt; Slide 11: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Misconception of One&#x27;s Own Greatness">Maling Pag-iisip sa Sariling Galing</span>
  [Current Image: images/gmrc_w1_img2.png]
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid thinking yonder that you have no talent or ability.">Iwasan ang pag-iisip na wala kang kakayahan o talento.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'I have no talent, I cannot do science subjects.'">Mali: 'Wala akong galing, hindi ko kaya ang science.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Every child has a unique strength waiting to be discovered.">Ang bawat bata ay may sariling galing na kailangang tuklasin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Maybe you just need practice and guidance from your teacher.">Maaaring kailangan mo lang ng pagsasanay at gabay ng guro.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Correct: 'I will practice to become good at science today.'">Tama: 'Magsasanay ako upang maging mahusay sa science.'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Self-confidence does not surrender at the very first try.">Ang tiwala sa sarili ay hindi sumusuko sa unang subok.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make sure your thoughts are positive in your writing today!">Tiyakin na positibo ang iyong kaisipan sa pagsusulat ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the key to success in everything you perform today!">Ito ang susi sa tagumpay sa lahat ng iyong ginagawa!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Thought Error: wrong: I&#x27;m not good -&gt; right: I will practice to learn">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Kaisipan Error: mali: wala akong galing -> tama: mag-eensayo ako upang matuto</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Thought Error">Kaisipan Error</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: I&#x27;m not good -&gt; right: I will practice to learn">mali: wala akong galing -> tama: mag-eensayo ako upang matuto</span>

Slide 12: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="False Boasting of Talent">Maling Pagyayabang ng Talento</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Avoid boasting or showing off when you are already skilled.">Iwasan ang pagmamayabang kapag ikaw ay mahusay na.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Wrong: 'I am better than all of you at reading books yonder!'">Mali: 'Mas magaling ako sa inyong lahat sa pagbasa!'</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Boasting does not display true and healthy self-confidence.">Ang pagyayabang ay hindi nagpapakita ng tiwala sa sarili.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="It displays lack of humility and respect for your classmates.">Ito ay nagpapakita ng kawalan ng kababaang-loob sa kapwa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The truly confident student serves others quietly in school.">Ang tunay na may tiwala ay tahimik na naglilingkod.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="He helps those who struggle without making them feel bad.">Tinutulungan niya ang mga nahihirapan nang walang yabang.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="This is the correct moral value taught in our GMRC class.">Ito ang wastong asal na itinuturo sa ating GMRC.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Be humble at all times and share your talents with others!">Maging mababa ang loob at palaging magbahagi ng biyaya!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Arrogant Error: wrong: show off in class -&gt; right: help with humility">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa Yabang Error: mali: magyabang sa klase -> tama: tumulong nang may kababaang-loob</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of HOTS Challenge: How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Halimbawa, tingnan natin ang tungkol sa HOTS Hamon: Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="To understand this concept deeply, we must look at how it applies to different situations in our daily lives.">Upang maunawaan ang konseptong ito nang malalim, kailangan nating tingnan kung paano ito nalalapat sa iba't ibang sitwasyon sa ating pang-araw-araw na buhay.</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Arrogant Error">Yabang Error</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="wrong: show off in class -&gt; right: help with humility">mali: magyabang sa klase -> tama: tumulong nang may kababaang-loob</span>
  Example: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="HOTS Challenge">HOTS Hamon</span>: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="How will you apply this concept to your daily decision-making?">Paano mo gagamitin ang konseptong ito sa iyong pang-araw-araw na pagpapasiya?</span>

Slide 13: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="The Self-Evaluation">Ang Pagtatasa sa Sariling Galing</span>
  Text: <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Let's check our own progress and development every day.">Suriin natin ang ating sariling pag-unlad araw-araw.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Make a written list of your hobbies and abilities today.">Gumawa ng listahan ng iyong mga hilig at kakayahan ngayon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Write down what practice routines you are doing at home.">Isulat kung anong mga pagsasanay ang iyong ginagawa.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="E.g., practicing refining drawings in the afternoon hours.">E.g., nag-eensayo ng pagpapakinis ng guhit sa hapon.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Self-assessment displays our personal discipline yonder.">Ang pagtatasa sa sarili ay nagpapakita ng disiplina natin.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="We find out where we still need to study and put in effort.">Nalalaman natin kung saan pa natin kailangang mag-aral.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Ask for guidance from your teacher or parents in this task.">Humingi ng tulong sa guro o magulang para sa pagsusuri.</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="Continue developing your own special talents in the community!">Ipagpatuloy ang pag-unlad ng iyong sariling talento ngayon!</span> <span class="fil-sentence" data-translation="For instance, consider the example of Assessment: Self-assessment: What am I good at?
